Me: Oh ok. I do have a last question. What could I do better next time when I'm approaching someone on the street, especially such an attractive lady like you are?

Me: But it was still too fast for you, right? When is the perfect time to give out my number?

Dear Dr. Shan,

We hope this email finds you well. We wanted to reach out to you regarding the solo audition that we had yesterday. We would like to express our sincerest apologies for not being as prepared as we could have been. Despite the lack of preparation, we put a lot of time and effort into this audition, and we hope that it was evident in our performance.

We are happy to inform you that Ryan will be playing the bass for our group, and although he was not able to record with us today, we are confident that he will figure it out in due time, since, even as you know, Ryan is an excellent musician, and we are lucky to have him as part of our group. We would also like to thank Caterina for beating us into shape and helping us with chords, harmonies, and rhythm (and eventually choreography as well.)

We have attached two videos of our best takes for your consideration. The first one is overall polished, while in the second one, we were less pressured, and some parts are better, while some are not. We wanted to provide you with both videos so you can get a sense of our group's capabilities.

We would also like to mention that we are one of the only male groups auditioning, and we hope that our group adds some diversity to the performance.

We apologize once again but also, thank you for your patience, time, and consideration. We look forward to hearing from you soon.

Sincerely,
The Fedora Tippers Group

aamindehkordi 02/12/2023 8:24 PM
This research paper focuses on the sexualization of female Twitch streamers, and the role of the male vs female gaze in this phenomenon. The paper examines the ways in which female Twitch streamers are sexualized by their male audience, and how this affects their experiences and identities as gamers and streamers. The paper also explores the wider context of online gaming communities and the sexualization of women in these spaces. Using a combination of academic literature, interviews with female Twitch streamers, and a survey of Twitch users, this paper argues that the sexualization of female Twitch streamers is a complex issue that is shaped by a variety of factors, including gender, technology, and gaming culture. The paper concludes by offering recommendations for how female Twitch streamers can resist and resist the sexualization, and for how the gaming industry and wider society can create more inclusive and respectful online gaming communities.
